Title Percutaneous Implantation of Infusion Port. right. 2. Procedure After skin preparation of right clavicular region on supine position, a 6 ml of 1% lidocaine HCI was locally infiltrated. The right internal jugular vein was punctured with a micropucture needle under US-guidance and a microsheath was then introduced into superior vena cava over a 0.018-inch hairwire. The skin was incised and subcutaneous pocket & tunnel was prepared by dissection. After dilation, an infusion port with catheter was inserted over a guidewire and a peel-away sheath. The tip of the catheter was adjusted at the atriocaval junction and the infusion port was filled with a 10 ml of saline solution mixed with Heparin 1.000 units for locking. The incision site was closed by applying tissue adhesive. The patient tolerated the procedure well and no immediate complication developed. [CONCLUSION] Uncomplicated implantation of infusion port via right transjugular venous approach under US & fluoroscopy. The right internal jugular vein was punctured with a micropucture needle under US-guidance and a microsheath was then introduced into superior vena cava over a 0.018-inch hairwire. Title Percutaneous Implantation of Infusion Port. right. 2. Procedure After skin preparation of right clavicular region on supine position, a 6 ml of 1% lidocaine HCI was locally infiltrated. The right internal jugular vein was punctured with a micropucture needle under US-guidance and a microsheath was then introduced into superior vena cava over a 0.018-inch hairwire. The skin was incised and subcutaneous pocket & tunnel was prepared by dissection. After dilation, an infusion port with catheter was inserted over a guidewire and a peel-away sheath. The tip of the catheter was adjusted at the atriocaval junction and the infusion port was filled with a 10 ml of saline solution mixed with Heparin 1.000 units for locking. The incision site was closed by applying tissue adhesive. The patient tolerated the procedure well and no immediate complication developed. [CONCLUSION] Uncomplicated implantation of infusion port via right transjugular venous approach under US & fluoroscopy. Title Percutaneous Implantation of Infusion Port. right. 2. Procedure After skin preparation of right clavicular region on supine position, a 6 ml of 1% lidocaine HCI was locally infiltrated. The right internal jugular vein was punctured with a micropucture needle under US-guidance and a microsheath was then introduced into superior vena cava over a 0.018-inch hairwire. The skin was incised and subcutaneous pocket & tunnel was prepared by dissection. After dilation, an infusion port with catheter was inserted over a guidewire and a peel-away sheath. The tip of the catheter was adjusted at the atriocaval junction and the infusion port was filled with a 10 ml of saline solution mixed with Heparin 1.000 units for locking. The incision site was closed by applying tissue adhesive. The patient tolerated the procedure well and no immediate complication developed. [CONCLUSION] Uncomplicated implantation of infusion port via right transjugular venous approach under US & fluoroscopy. 내원일: 2025.02.10
내원사유: 정기 진료
진단명: 미확인
중증도: 경미

[2025.02.13] [별지 제1호 서식] 진료비 세부산정내역 서식 (제2조제1항 관련) 환자등록번호
내원일: 2025.02.13
내원사유: 정기 진료
진단명: 미확인
처방: 내역 등이 확인되므로 원칙적으로 환자 본인 외에 발급을 금합니다. 다만, 본 세부내역서 발급에 대해 별도로 환자 본인으로부터 위임을 받은 것이 확인된 자 또는 법정대리인에겐 발급이 가능합니다. 2. 비고란은 세부산정내역을 발부하는 영수증번호 등 요양기관이 필요한 경우 추가 기재하는 공간으로 활용할 수 있습니다. 3. 동 서식에 명시된 항목은 「국민건강보험 요양급여의 기준에 관한 규칙」 제7조제3항에 따라 필수 기재되어야 합니다. 5/5 대표자 윤승규 병원 [별지 제1호 서식] 진료비 세부산정내역 서식 (제2조제1항 관련) 환자등록번호
특이사항: 란은 세부산정내역을 발부하는 영수증번호 등 요양기관이 필요한 경우 추가 기재하는 공간으로 활용할 수 있습니다. 3. 동 서식에 명시된 항목은 「국민건강보험 요양급여의 기준에 관한 규칙」 제7조제3항에 따라 필수 기재되어야 합니다. 5/5 대표자 윤승규 병원 [별지 제1호 서식] 진료비 세부산정내역 서식 (제2조제1항 관련) 환자등록번호

[2025.02.13] 일반사항 안내 1. 진료비 계산서·영수증의 세부내역서는 환자의 구체적인 처방 내역 등이 확인되므로 원칙적으로 환자 본인 외에 발급을 금합니다. 다만, 본 세부내역서 발급에 대해 별도로 환자 본인으로부터 위임을 받은 것이 확인된 자 또는 법정대리인에겐 발급이 가능합니다. 2. 비고란은 세부산정내역을 발부하는 영수증번호 등 요양기관이 필요한 경우 추가 기재하는 공간으로 활용할 수 있습니다. 3. 동 서식에 명시된 항목은 「국민건강보험 요양급여의 기준에 관한 규칙」 제7조제3항에 따라 필수 기재되어야 합니다. 5/5 대표자 윤승규 [별지 제1호 서식] 진료비 세부산정내역 서식 (제2조제1항 관련) 환자등록번호 환자성명
내원일: 2025.02.13
내원사유: 정기 진료
